  <script type="text/javascript">

    function submitZipCodeForm(form, zipcodeValue)
    {
      if (isValidZipCodeFormat(zipcodeValue))
      {
        //save the zipcode
        $.cookie('cvStoreZipCode', zipcodeValue);
      }
      else
      {
        //delete the cookie if zipcode is not valid
        $.cookie('cvStoreZipCode', null);
      }

      form.submit();
    }

    //valid zip code format is 5 digit number
    function isValidZipCodeFormat(val)
    {
      //check if 5 digits
      if (val.length != 5)
      {
        return false;
      }
      //checks if positive whole number
      for (var i = 0; i < val.length; i++)
      {
        var ch = val.charAt(i);
        if (ch < "0" || ch > "9")
        {
          return false;
        }
      }
      return true;
    }

    $(document).ready(function(){
      //IE6 PNG FIX
      //$('#header-top, button, #header-loc, #home-area').supersleight({shim: '/wcsstore/CVB2BDirectStorefrontAssetStore/javascript/blank.gif'});
      //Sprint3 -- Type ahead implementation -- start
        $("html").click(function() {
            $("#type-ahead-container").hide();
        });
        //Then override that on your #wndSL's click event using .stopPropagation();

        $("#type-ahead-container").click(function (event) {
          event.stopPropagation();
          $('#type-ahead-container').css("display", "block");
        });
        $("#type-ahead-search").click(function (event) {
          var style = $("#type-ahead-container").css("display");
          if(style == "block") {
            event.stopPropagation();
            $('#type-ahead-container').css("display", "block");
          } else {
            $('#type-ahead-container').css("display", "none");
          }
        });
      //Sprint3 -- Type ahead implementation -- end

        $("#cat-nav li").hover(
            function(){ $("ul",this).addClass("sfHover").show(); },

        if($('#search-box input[type=text]').val() != "" && $('#search-box input[type=text]').val() != 'Enter Keyword or Item #' ) {

          return false
        }

    	<script type="text/javascript">
        	//Sprint3 -- Typeahead fix for placeholder attribute in IE
        function testAttribute(element, attribute){
        
              var test = document.createElement(element);
              if (attribute in test) {
                $('#type-ahead-search').focus();
                $('#pop-back-search').hide();
                return true;
              }
              else
                return false;
            }
          if (!testAttribute("input", "placeholder")){
          	$(window).load(function(){  
				var demo = document.getElementById("type-ahead-search");
              	//var text_content = searchStatictext;
              	if(demo.value == ""){
              		demo.value = searchStatictext;
              	} 
              	$('#pop-back-search').hide();
              	demo.onfocus = function() {
                	if (this.value == searchStatictext){
                 		this.value = "";
                	}
              	}
              	demo.onblur = function() {
                	if (this.value == ""){
                    	this.value = searchStatictext;
                	}
              	}
			}); 
            
          }
        //Sprint3 -- Typeahead fix for placeholder attribute in IE
      </script>

	$(document).ready(function() {
      // Mini account hover functionality
      $('.site.header div.account').hover(
        function(){ // handlerIn
          $('div.account .contents').stop().delay(132).fadeIn(0, function(){ // First stop the animation queue, then delay, then fade
            $('.account .edit.link, .account .icon, .account .bug, .account.hover-container').addClass('hover'); // Restores account area and icon to regular state
          });
        },
        function(){ // handlerOut
          $('div.account .contents').stop().delay(132).fadeOut(0, function(){ // First stop the animation queue, then delay, then fade
            $('.account .edit.link, .account .icon, .account .bug, .account.hover-container').removeClass('hover'); // Restores account area and icon to regular state
          });
        }
      ); // End account hover functionality

      // Live assistance hover functionality
      $('.site.header .column.two .hover-container').hover(
        function(){ // handlerIn
          $('.column.two .hover-container .contents').fadeIn(); // Toggles the live assistance contents
        },
        function(){ // handlerOut
          $('.column.two .hover-container .contents').fadeOut(); // Toggles the mini live assistance contents
        }
      ); // End live assistance hover functionality
      
	});

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

var mouseOverFlag;

	function getMiniCartDetails()
	{	
		var startTime = new Date().getTime();
		var ajaxOptions = {
				   type: "GET",
				   dataType: "html",
				   timeout:30000, //30 sec timeout
				   url: "/webapp/wcs/stores/servlet/MiniShopBagAJAXView",
				   data: "catalogId=" + 10051 + "&storeId=" + 10151 + "&langId=" + -1,
				   success: function(html){
				   		var endTime = new Date().getTime();
			  	   		var delayTime = 132 - (endTime - startTime);
			  	   		
			  	   		if(delayTime < 0){
			  	   			delayTime = 0;
			  	   		}
			  	   		
						$("#mini-bag-popUp").html(html);
						
						$('div.mini.cart .contents').stop().delay(delayTime).fadeIn(0, function(){ // First stop the animation queue, then delay, then fade
							$('.mini.cart .edit.link, .mini.cart .icon, .mini.cart .bug, .mini.cart.hover-container').addClass('hover'); // Restores cart area and icon to regular state
          				});
          				
          				//In case the user has already moved the mouse out 
						if(!mouseOverFlag){
						 $('div.mini.cart .contents').stop().delay(132).fadeOut(0, function(){ // First stop the animation queue, then delay, then fade
				            $('.mini.cart .edit.link, .mini.cart .icon, .mini.cart .bug, .mini.cart.hover-container').removeClass('hover'); // Restores cart area and icon to regular state
				          });
						}
          				
          				//  Get records from RR 
						rrTag.getMiniCartRecs();
						
			  		},
			  	   error: function(){
			  	   
						$("#mini-bag-popUp").html('<div class="contents"><div class="all-products"><h3 class="headline">My Cart</h3><div class="product"><p>We are unable to load the cart at this time.</p></div><hr></div></div>');
						$('div.mini.cart .contents').stop().delay(132).fadeIn(0, function(){ // First stop the animation queue, then delay, then fade
            				$('.mini.cart .edit.link, .mini.cart .icon, .mini.cart .bug, .mini.cart.hover-container').addClass('hover'); // Restores cart area and icon to regular state
          				});
			  		}
			   };
		  if ($('#mini-bag-popUp').is(':empty')) {
		  $.ajax(ajaxOptions);
		  setInterval(function() {$('#scroll-pane').jScrollPane();}, 1);
		  }
		  return false;
	}
  
	$(document).ready(function() {
		// Mini cart hover functionality
      $('.site.header div.mini.cart').hover(
        function(){ // handlerIn
        	mouseOverFlag = true;
        	
        	//getMiniCartDetails();
        },
        function(){ // handlerOut
          mouseOverFlag = false;
          $('div.mini.cart .contents').stop().delay(132).fadeOut(0, function(){ // First stop the animation queue, then delay, then fade
            $('.mini.cart .edit.link, .mini.cart .icon, .mini.cart .bug, .mini.cart.hover-container').removeClass('hover'); // Restores cart area and icon to regular state
            $("#mini-bag-popUp").empty();
          });
          
        }
      ); // End cart hover functionality
     
	});
	
	(function($) {
	$.extend({ 
		uiLock: function(content){
			if(content == 'undefined') content = '';
			$('<div></div>').attr('id', 'uiLockId').css({
				'position': 'absolute',
				'top': 0,
				'left': 0,
				'z-index': 9999,
				'opacity': 0.0,
				'width':'100%',
				'height':'100%',
				'color':'white',
				'background-color':'white'
			}).html(content).appendTo('body');
		},
		uiUnlock: function(){
			$('#uiLockId').remove();
		}
	});
})(jQuery);
	
	function submitRequest(form, isCheckout) {
    	$.uiLock('');  
    	$("#checkoutLink").val(isCheckout);
        form.submit();
    }

      $.uiLock('');
    }

<script>
var here = window.location + ""; 
function ea_updateRowsPerPage( ele )
{
      var here = window.location + "";
      if(here.match(/searchTerm/)){
          /searchTerm=([^&]*)/.exec(here);
          searchTerm = RegExp.$1;
    	  window.location = ( "_/N-0/Ntk-Search_All/Ntt-"+searchTerm+"/Rpp-"+ ele.value);
      }else if(here.match(/Rpp-\d/)){
            window.location = here.replace(/Rpp-\d/g, "Rpp-"+ ele.value);
      }else if(here.match(/\?/)){
            window.location = here.replace(/\?/g, "/Rpp-"+ ele.value +"?"); 
      }else if(here.match(/#/)) {
  	  		window.location = here.replace(/#/g, "/Rpp-"+ ele.value +"#");
	  }else{
        	window.location += "/Rpp-"+ ele.value
      }
}

var resPerPage = /Rpp-(\d)/.exec(here);
try{
	$('[name=Rpp]').val(resPerPage[1]);
}catch(e){
    $('[name=Rpp]').val('1');
}     
</script>

<script>
var here = window.location + ""; 
function ea_updateRowsPerPage( ele )
{
      var here = window.location + "";
      if(here.match(/searchTerm/)){
          /searchTerm=([^&]*)/.exec(here);
          searchTerm = RegExp.$1;
    	  window.location = ( "_/N-0/Ntk-Search_All/Ntt-"+searchTerm+"/Rpp-"+ ele.value);
      }else if(here.match(/Rpp-\d/)){
            window.location = here.replace(/Rpp-\d/g, "Rpp-"+ ele.value);
      }else if(here.match(/\?/)){
            window.location = here.replace(/\?/g, "/Rpp-"+ ele.value +"?"); 
      }else if(here.match(/#/)) {
  	  		window.location = here.replace(/#/g, "/Rpp-"+ ele.value +"#");
	  }else{
        	window.location += "/Rpp-"+ ele.value
      }
}

var resPerPage = /Rpp-(\d)/.exec(here);
try{
	$('[name=Rpp]').val(resPerPage[1]);
}catch(e){
    $('[name=Rpp]').val('1');
}     
</script>
